</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-
style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">This Opinion Letter is 
furnished to you in connection with your Registration Statement on Form S-3 (as 
amended or supplemented, the &#8220;<font style="text-
decoration:underline;">Registration Statement</font>&#8221;) filed with the 
Securities and Exchange Commission (the &#8220;<font style="text-
decoration:underline;">Commission</font>&#8221;) under the Securities Act of 
1933, as amended (the &#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Securities
Act</font>&#8221;), relating to the registration of the offering by Earthstone 
Energy, Inc., a Delaware corporation (the &#8220;<font style="text-
decoration:underline;">Company</font>&#8221;) of an indeterminate number of 
(i)&#160;shares of Common Stock, par value $0.001 per share of the Company (the 
&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Common Stock</font>&#8221;), 
(ii)&#160;shares of Preferred Stock of the Company (the &#8220;<font 
style="text-decoration:underline;">Preferred Stock</font>&#8221;), 
(iii)&#160;senior and subordinated debt securities (the &#8220;<font 
style="text-decoration:underline;">Debt Securities</font>&#8221;), (iv) rights 
to purchase common stock or other securities (the &#8220;<font style="text-
decoration:underline;">Rights</font>&#8221;), (v)&#160;warrants to purchase 
Common Stock and Preferred Stock (the &#8220;<font style="text-
decoration:underline;">Warrants</font>&#8221;), (vi) units consisting of two or 
more of the foregoing securities (&#8220;<font style="text-
decoration:underline;">Units</font>&#8221;), and (vii) guarantees of Debt 
Securities (&#8220;<font style="text-
decoration:underline;">Guarantees</font>&#8221;) by one or more of the 
guarantors identified in <font style="text-decoration:underline;">Exhibit 
A</font> hereto (each, a &#8220;<font style="text-
decoration:underline;">Guarantor</font>&#8221;) having a maximum aggregate 
public offering price of $300,000,000. The Registration Statement provides that 
the Common Stock, Preferred Stock, Debt Securities, Rights, Warrants, Units and 
Guarantees may be sold from time to time in one or more offerings up to a total 
public offering price of $300,000,000 on terms to be set forth in one or more 
prospectus supplements (each, a &#8220;<font style="text-
decoration:underline;">Prospectus Supplement</font>&#8221;) to the prospectus 
contained in the Registration Statement. </p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-
style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">We have reviewed such 
documents and made such examination of law as we have deemed necessary or 
appropriate to give the opinions expressed below. We have relied, without 
independent verification, on certificates of public officials and, as to matters
of fact material to the opinions set forth below, on certificates of officers of
the Company and the Guarantors. </p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-
style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">We express no opinion as
to the laws of any jurisdiction other than any published constitutions, 
treaties, laws, rules or regulations or judicial or administrative decisions 
(&#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Laws</font>&#8221;) of 
(i)&#160;the federal Laws of the United States, (ii)&#160;the Laws of the State 
of Delaware, (iii) the Laws of the State of New York, and (iv) the Laws of the 
State of Texas. </p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-
style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">This Opinion Letter is 
limited to the matters stated herein, and no opinion is implied or may be 
inferred beyond the matters expressly stated.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-
style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">For purposes of the 
opinions expressed in paragraphs (1)&#160;through (7)&#160;below, without 
limiting any other exceptions or qualifications set forth herein, we have 
assumed that after the issuance of the Common Stock offered pursuant to the 
Registration Statement, the total number of issued shares of Common Stock, 
together with the total number of shares of Common Stock reserved for issuance 
upon the exercise, exchange or conversion, as the case may be, of any 
exercisable, exchangeable or convertible security then outstanding, will not 
exceed the total number of authorized shares of Common Stock under the 
Company&#8217;s Certificate of Incorporation, as amended and then in effect. 
</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-
indent:0%;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-
style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">For purposes of the 
opinions expressed in paragraphs (1)&#160;through (7)&#160;below, without 
limiting any other exceptions or qualifications set forth herein, we have also 
assumed that after the issuance of the Preferred Stock offered pursuant to the 
Registration Statement, the total number of issued shares of Preferred Stock, 
together with the total number of shares of Preferred Stock reserved for 
issuance upon the exercise, exchange or conversion of any exercisable, 
exchangeable or convertible security then outstanding, will not exceed the total
number of authorized shares of Preferred Stock under the Company&#8217;s 
Certificate of Incorporation, as amended and then in effect, and that the 
Company will not create a series of Preferred Stock that is assessable.</p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-

and subject to the limitations, qualifications, exceptions and assumptions set 
forth herein, it is our opinion that:  </p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-

for issuance by the Board of Directors of the Company or a duly authorized
committee thereof (the &#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Common 
Stock Authorizing Resolution</font>&#8221;) and (ii)&#160;shares of Common Stock

Stock have been issued as contemplated in the Preferred Stock Authorizing 
Resolution against receipt by the Company of the consideration therefor provided
for in the Preferred Stock Authorizing Resolution, then (A)&#160;the Preferred 
Stock will be validly issued, fully paid and non-assessable and (B)&#160;if the 
Preferred Stock is convertible into Common Stock, the Common Stock, if and when 
duly issued upon the conversion of such Preferred Stock, will be validly issued,
fully paid and non-assessable.</p></td></tr></table></div>

amended (the &#8220;<font style="text-decoration:underline;">Trust Indenture 
Act</font>&#8221;), (iii)&#160;the trustee under the applicable indenture has 
been duly qualified under the Trust Indenture Act, (iv) the terms of the Debt 
Securities and of their issuance and sale have been duly established in 
conformity with the applicable indenture so as not to violate any law or result 
in any default under or breach of any agreement or instrument binding upon the 
Company and so as to comply with any requirement or restriction imposed by any 
court or governmental body having jurisdiction over the Company, (v)&#160;any 
shares of Common Stock issuable upon conversion of the Debt Securities, if 
applicable, have been duly and validly authorized for issuance, (vi) the Debt 
Securities have been duly executed and authenticated in accordance with the 
applicable indenture and (vii)&#160;the Debt Securities have been issued as 
contemplated in the Debt Securities Authorizing Resolution against receipt by
the Company of the consideration therefor provided in the Debt Securities 
Authorizing Resolution, then (A)&#160;the Debt Securities will constitute valid 
and legally binding obligations of the Company and (B)&#160;if the Debt 
Securities are convertible into Common Stock, the Common Stock, if and when 
issued upon conversion of the Debt Securities will be validly issued, fully paid
and non-assessable.</p></td></tr></table></div>
